<h2 id="examples" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#examples"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Examples</h2>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4bhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4bhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4bhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="controlled-size" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#controlled-size"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Controlled size</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To control the size of the floating panel programmatically, you can pass the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">size</code> <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onResize</code> prop to the machine.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4hhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4hhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4hhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="controlled-position" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#controlled-position"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Controlled position</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To control the position of the floating panel programmatically, you can pass the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">position</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onPositionChange</code> prop
to the machine.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4nhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4nhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4nhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="anchor-position" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#anchor-position"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Anchor Position</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">getAnchorPosition</code> function to compute the initial position of the floating panel. This function is called when
the panel is opened and receives the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">triggerRect</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">boundaryRect</code>.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4thanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4thanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4thanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="open-state" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#open-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Open State</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To control the open state of the floating panel programmatically, you can pass the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">open</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onOpenChange</code> prop to the
machine.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_53hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_53hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_53hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="lazy-mount" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#lazy-mount"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Lazy Mount</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To lazy mount the floating panel, you can pass the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">lazyMount</code> prop to the machine.</p>

<h3 id="context" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Context</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To access the context of the floating panel, you can use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useFloatingPanelContext</code> hook or the
<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">FloatingPanel.Context</code> component.</p>

<h2 id="api-reference" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#api-reference"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>API Reference</h2>

          \u003c/FloatingPanel.StageTrigger\u003e\n                \u003cFloatingPanel.CloseTrigger class={styles.ControlButton}\u003e\n                  \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n                \u003c/FloatingPanel.CloseTrigger\u003e\n              \u003c/FloatingPanel.Control\u003e\n            \u003c/FloatingPanel.Header\u003e\n          \u003c/FloatingPanel.DragTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.Body class={styles.Body}\u003e\n            \u003cp\u003eSome content\u003c/p\u003e\n          \u003c/FloatingPanel.Body\u003e\n\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"n\" class={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"e\" class={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"w\" class={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"s\" class={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"ne\" class={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"se\" class={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"sw\" class={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"nw\" class={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n        \u003c/FloatingPanel.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/FloatingPanel.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Portal\u003e\n  \u003c/FloatingPanel.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { FloatingPanel } from the `size` `onResize` prop to the machine.\n\n**Example: controlled-size**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { FloatingPanel } from '@ark-ui/react/floating-panel'\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport { ArrowDownLeft, GripVertical, Maximize2, Minus, XIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport styles from 'styles/floating-panel.module.css'\n\nexport const ControlledSize = () =\u003e {\n  const [size, setSize] = useState({ width: 400, height: 300 })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cFloatingPanel.Root size={size} onSizeChange={(e) =\u003e setSize(e.size)}\u003e\n      \u003cFloatingPanel.Trigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003eToggle Panel\u003c/FloatingPanel.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cPortal\u003e\n        \u003cFloatingPanel.Positioner className={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.Content className={styles.Content}\u003e\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.DragTrigger\u003e\n              \u003cFloatingPanel.Header className={styles.Header}\u003e\n                \u003cFloatingPanel.Title className={styles.Title}\u003e\n                  \u003cGripVertical /\u003e\n                  Floating Panel\n                \u003c/FloatingPanel.Title\u003e\n                \u003cFloatingPanel.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n                  \u003cFloatingPanel.StageTrigger stage=\"minimized\" className={styles.ControlButton}\u003e\n                    \u003cMinus /\u003e\n                  \u003c/FloatingPanel.StageTrigger\u003e\n                  \u003cFloatingPanel.StageTrigger stage=\"maximized\" className={styles.ControlButton}\u003e\n                    \u003cMaximize2 /\u003e\n                  \u003c/FloatingPanel.StageTrigger\u003e\n                  \u003cFloatingPanel.StageTrigger stage=\"default\" className={styles.ControlButton}\u003e\n                    \u003cArrowDownLeft /\u003e\n                  \u003c/FloatingPanel.StageTrigger\u003e\n                  \u003cFloatingPanel.CloseTrigger className={styles.ControlButton}\u003e\n                    \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n                  \u003c/FloatingPanel.CloseTrigger\u003e\n                \u003c/FloatingPanel.Control\u003e\n              \u003c/FloatingPanel.Header\u003e\n            \u003c/FloatingPanel.DragTrigger\u003e\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.Body className={styles.Body}\u003e\n              \u003cp\u003eSome content\u003c/p\u003e\n            \u003c/FloatingPanel.Body\u003e\n\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"n\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"e\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"w\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"s\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"ne\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"se\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"sw\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"nw\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n          \u003c/FloatingPanel.Content\u003e\n        \u003c/FloatingPanel.Positioner\u003e\n      \u003c/Portal\u003e\n    \u003c/FloatingPanel.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { FloatingPanel } from '@ark-ui/solid/floating-panel'\nimport { ArrowDownLeft, GripVertical, Maximize2, Minus, XIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { createSignal } from 'solid-js'\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport styles from 'styles/floating-panel.module.css'\n\nexport const ControlledSize = () =\u003e {\n  const [size, setSize] = createSignal({ width: 400, height: 300 })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cFloatingPanel.Root size={size()} onSizeChange={(e) =\u003e setSize(e.size)}\u003e\n      \u003cFloatingPanel.Trigger \u003cFloatingPanel.Title class={styles.Title}\u003e\n                  \u003cGripVertical /\u003e\n                  Floating Panel\n                \u003c/FloatingPanel.Title\u003e\n                \u003cFloatingPanel.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n                  \u003cFloatingPanel.StageTrigger stage=\"minimized\" class={styles.ControlButton}\u003e\n                    \u003cMinus /\u003e\n                  \u003c/FloatingPanel.StageTrigger\u003e\n                  \u003cFloatingPanel.StageTrigger stage=\"maximized\" class={styles.ControlButton}\u003e\n                    \u003cMaximize2 /\u003e\n                  \u003c/FloatingPanel.StageTrigger\u003e\n                  \u003cFloatingPanel.StageTrigger stage=\"default\" class={styles.ControlButton}\u003e\n                    \u003cArrowDownLeft /\u003e\n                  \u003c/FloatingPanel.StageTrigger\u003e\n                  \u003cFloatingPanel.CloseTrigger class={styles.ControlButton}\u003e\n                    \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n                  \u003c/FloatingPanel.CloseTrigger\u003e\n                \u003c/FloatingPanel.Control\u003e\n              \u003c/FloatingPanel.Header\u003e\n            \u003c/FloatingPanel.DragTrigger\u003e\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.Body class={styles.Body}\u003e\n              \u003cp\u003eSome content\u003c/p\u003e\n            \u003c/FloatingPanel.Body\u003e\n\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"n\" class={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"e\" class={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"ne\" class={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"se\" class={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"sw\" class={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"nw\" class={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n          \u003c/FloatingPanel.Content\u003e\n        \u003c/FloatingPanel.Positioner\u003e\n      \u003c/Portal\u003e\n    \u003c/FloatingPanel.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { FloatingPanel } from '@ark-ui/vue/floating-panel'\nimport { ArrowDownLeft, GripVertical, Maximize2, Minus, XIcon } \u003c/FloatingPanel.Positioner\u003e\n  \u003c/Portal\u003e\n\u003c/FloatingPanel.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Controlled position\n\nTo control the position of the floating panel programmatically, you can pass the `position` and `onPositionChange` prop\nto the machine.\n\n**Example: controlled-position**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { FloatingPanel } from '@ark-ui/react/floating-panel'\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport { ArrowDownLeft, GripVertical, Maximize2, Minus, XIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport styles from 'styles/floating-panel.module.css'\n\nexport const ControlledPosition = () =\u003e {\n  const [position, setPosition] = useState({ x: 200, y: 200 })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cFloatingPanel.Root position={position} onPositionChange={(e) =\u003e setPosition(e.position)}\u003e\n      \u003cFloatingPanel.Trigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003eToggle Panel\u003c/FloatingPanel.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cPortal\u003e\n        \u003cFloatingPanel.Positioner className={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.Content className={styles.Content}\u003e\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.DragTrigger\u003e\n              \u003cFloatingPanel.Header className={styles.Header}\u003e\n                \u003cFloatingPanel.Title className={styles.Title}\u003e\n                  \u003cGripVertical /\u003e\n                  Floating Panel\n                \u003c/FloatingPanel.Title\u003e\n                \u003cFloatingPanel.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n                  \u003cFloatingPanel.StageTrigger stage=\"minimized\" className={styles.ControlButton}\u003e\n                    \u003cMinus /\u003e\n                  \u003c/FloatingPanel.StageTrigger\u003e\n                  \u003cFloatingPanel.StageTrigger stage=\"maximized\" className={styles.ControlButton}\u003e\n                    \u003cMaximize2 /\u003e\n                  \u003c/FloatingPanel.StageTrigger\u003e\n                  \u003cFloatingPanel.StageTrigger stage=\"default\" className={styles.ControlButton}\u003e\n                    \u003cArrowDownLeft /\u003e\n                  \u003c/FloatingPanel.StageTrigger\u003e\n                  \u003cFloatingPanel.CloseTrigger className={styles.ControlButton}\u003e\n                    \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n                  \u003c/FloatingPanel.CloseTrigger\u003e\n                \u003c/FloatingPanel.Control\u003e\n              \u003c/FloatingPanel.Header\u003e\n            \u003c/FloatingPanel.DragTrigger\u003e\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.Body className={styles.Body}\u003e\n              \u003cp\u003eSome content\u003c/p\u003e\n            \u003c/FloatingPanel.Body\u003e\n\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"n\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"e\" Position\n\nUse the `getAnchorPosition` function to compute the initial position of the floating panel. This function is called when\nthe panel is opened and receives the `triggerRect` and `boundaryRect`.\n\n**Example: anchor-position**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { FloatingPanel } from '@ark-ui/react/floating-panel'\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport { ArrowDownLeft, GripVertical, Maximize2, Minus, XIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/floating-panel.module.css'\n\nexport const AnchorPosition = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cFloatingPanel.Root\n    getAnchorPosition={({ triggerRect }) =\u003e {\n      if (!triggerRect) return { x: 0, y: 0 }\n      return {\n        x: triggerRect.x + triggerRect.width / 2,\n        y: triggerRect.y + triggerRect.height / 2,\n      }\n    }}\n  \u003e\n    \u003cFloatingPanel.Trigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003eToggle Panel\u003c/FloatingPanel.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cPortal\u003e\n      \u003cFloatingPanel.Positioner className={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n        \u003cFloatingPanel.Content className={styles.Content}\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.DragTrigger\u003e\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.Header className={styles.Header}\u003e\n              \u003cFloatingPanel.Title className={styles.Title}\u003e\n                \u003cGripVertical /\u003e\n                Floating Panel\n              \u003c/FloatingPanel.Title\u003e\n              \u003cFloatingPanel.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n                \u003cFloatingPanel.StageTrigger stage=\"minimized\" className={styles.ControlButton}\u003e\n                  \u003cMinus /\u003e\n                \u003c/FloatingPanel.StageTrigger\u003e\n                \u003cFloatingPanel.StageTrigger stage=\"maximized\" className={styles.ControlButton}\u003e\n                  \u003cMaximize2 /\u003e\n                \u003c/FloatingPanel.StageTrigger\u003e\n                \u003cFloatingPanel.StageTrigger stage=\"default\" className={styles.ControlButton}\u003e\n                  \u003cArrowDownLeft /\u003e\n                \u003c/FloatingPanel.StageTrigger\u003e\n                \u003cFloatingPanel.CloseTrigger className={styles.ControlButton}\u003e\n                  \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n                \u003c/FloatingPanel.CloseTrigger\u003e\n              \u003c/FloatingPanel.Control\u003e\n            \u003c/FloatingPanel.Header\u003e\n          \u003c/FloatingPanel.DragTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.Body className={styles.Body}\u003e\n            \u003cp\u003eSome content\u003c/p\u003e\n          \u003c/FloatingPanel.Body\u003e\n\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"n\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"e\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"w\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"s\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"ne\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"se\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"sw\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"nw\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n        \u003c/FloatingPanel.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/FloatingPanel.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Portal\u003e\n  \u003c/FloatingPanel.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { FloatingPanel } from '@ark-ui/solid/floating-panel'\nimport { ArrowDownLeft, GripVertical, Maximize2, Minus, XIcon } from Maximize2, Minus, XIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/floating-panel.module.css'\n\ninterface Rect {\n  x: number\n  y: number\n  width: number\n  height: number\n}\n\ninterface AnchorPositionDetails {\n  triggerRect: Rect | null\n  boundaryRect: Rect | null\n}\n\nconst getAnchorPosition = ({ triggerRect }: AnchorPositionDetails) =\u003e {\n  if (!triggerRect) return { x: 0, y: 0 }\n  return {\n    x: triggerRect.x + triggerRect.width / 2,\n    y: triggerRect.y + triggerRect.height / 2,\n  }\n}\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cFloatingPanel.Root \u003cFloatingPanel.StageTrigger stage=\"minimized\" class={styles.ControlButton}\u003e\n                \u003cMinus /\u003e\n              \u003c/FloatingPanel.StageTrigger\u003e\n              \u003cFloatingPanel.StageTrigger stage=\"maximized\" class={styles.ControlButton}\u003e\n                \u003cMaximize2 /\u003e\n              \u003c/FloatingPanel.StageTrigger\u003e\n              \u003cFloatingPanel.StageTrigger stage=\"default\" class={styles.ControlButton}\u003e\n                \u003cArrowDownLeft /\u003e\n              \u003c/FloatingPanel.StageTrigger\u003e\n              \u003cFloatingPanel.CloseTrigger class={styles.ControlButton}\u003e\n                \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/FloatingPanel.CloseTrigger\u003e\n            \u003c/FloatingPanel.Control\u003e\n          \u003c/FloatingPanel.Header\u003e\n        \u003c/FloatingPanel.DragTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cFloatingPanel.Body class={styles.Body}\u003e\n          \u003cp\u003eSome content\u003c/p\u003e\n          \u003cp\u003eAnchored to trigger center\u003c/p\u003e\n        \u003c/FloatingPanel.Body\u003e\n\n        \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"n\" class={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n        \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"e\" class={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n        \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"w\" class={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n        \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"s\" class={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n        \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"ne\" class={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n        \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"se\" class={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n        \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"sw\" class={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n        \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"nw\" class={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n      \u003c/FloatingPanel.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/FloatingPanel.Positioner\u003e\n  \u003c/Portal\u003e\n\u003c/FloatingPanel.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Open State\n\nTo control the open state of the floating panel programmatically, you can pass the `open` and `onOpenChange` prop to the\nmachine.\n\n**Example: controlled-open**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { FloatingPanel } from '@ark-ui/react/floating-panel'\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport { ArrowDownLeft, GripVertical, Maximize2, Minus, XIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport styles from 'styles/floating-panel.module.css'\n\nexport const ControlledOpen = () =\u003e {\n  const [open, setOpen] = useState(false)\n\n  return (\n    \u003cFloatingPanel.Root open={open} onOpenChange={(e) =\u003e setOpen(e.open)}\u003e\n      \u003cFloatingPanel.Trigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003eToggle Panel\u003c/FloatingPanel.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cPortal\u003e\n        \u003cFloatingPanel.Positioner className={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.Content className={styles.Content}\u003e\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.DragTrigger\u003e\n              \u003cFloatingPanel.Header className={styles.Header}\u003e\n                \u003cFloatingPanel.Title className={styles.Title}\u003e\n                  \u003cGripVertical /\u003e\n                  Floating Panel\n                \u003c/FloatingPanel.Title\u003e\n                \u003cFloatingPanel.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n                  \u003cFloatingPanel.StageTrigger stage=\"minimized\" className={styles.ControlButton}\u003e\n                    \u003cMinus /\u003e\n                  \u003c/FloatingPanel.StageTrigger\u003e\n                  \u003cFloatingPanel.StageTrigger stage=\"maximized\" className={styles.ControlButton}\u003e\n                    \u003cMaximize2 /\u003e\n                  \u003c/FloatingPanel.StageTrigger\u003e\n                  \u003cFloatingPanel.StageTrigger stage=\"default\" className={styles.ControlButton}\u003e\n                    \u003cArrowDownLeft /\u003e\n                  \u003c/FloatingPanel.StageTrigger\u003e\n                  \u003cFloatingPanel.CloseTrigger className={styles.ControlButton}\u003e\n                    \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n                  \u003c/FloatingPanel.CloseTrigger\u003e\n                \u003c/FloatingPanel.Control\u003e\n              \u003c/FloatingPanel.Header\u003e\n            \u003c/FloatingPanel.DragTrigger\u003e\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.Body className={styles.Body}\u003e\n              \u003cp\u003eSome content\u003c/p\u003e\n            \u003c/FloatingPanel.Body\u003e\n\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"n\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"e\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"w\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"s\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"ne\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"se\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"sw\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"nw\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n          \u003c/FloatingPanel.Content\u003e\n        \u003c/FloatingPanel.Positioner\u003e\n      \u003c/Portal\u003e\n    \u003c/FloatingPanel.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { FloatingPanel } from '@ark-ui/solid/floating-panel'\nimport { ArrowDownLeft, GripVertical, Maximize2, Minus, XIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { createSignal } from 'solid-js'\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport styles from 'styles/floating-panel.module.css'\n\nexport const ControlledOpen = () =\u003e {\n  const [open, setOpen] = createSignal(false)\n\n  return (\n    \u003cFloatingPanel.Root open={open()} onOpenChange={(e) =\u003e setOpen(e.open)}\u003e\n      \u003cFloatingPanel.Trigger class={styles.Trigger}\u003eToggle Panel\u003c/FloatingPanel.Trigger\u003e\n \u003cFloatingPanel.DragTrigger\u003e\n              \u003cFloatingPanel.Header class={styles.Header}\u003e\n                \u003cFloatingPanel.Title class={styles.Title}\u003e\n                  \u003cGripVertical /\u003e\n                  Floating Panel\n                \u003c/FloatingPanel.Title\u003e\n                \u003cFloatingPanel.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n                  \u003cFloatingPanel.StageTrigger stage=\"minimized\" class={styles.ControlButton}\u003e\n                    \u003cMinus /\u003e\n                  \u003c/FloatingPanel.StageTrigger\u003e\n                  \u003cFloatingPanel.StageTrigger stage=\"maximized\" class={styles.ControlButton}\u003e\n                    \u003cMaximize2 /\u003e\n             \u003c/FloatingPanel.StageTrigger\u003e\n                  \u003cFloatingPanel.CloseTrigger class={styles.ControlButton}\u003e\n                    \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n                  \u003c/FloatingPanel.CloseTrigger\u003e\n                \u003c/FloatingPanel.Control\u003e\n              \u003c/FloatingPanel.Header\u003e\n            \u003c/FloatingPanel.DragTrigger\u003e\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.Body class={styles.Body}\u003e\n              \u003cp\u003eSome content\u003c/p\u003e\n            \u003c/FloatingPanel.Body\u003e\n\n \u003c/Portal\u003e\n\u003c/FloatingPanel.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Lazy Mount\n\nTo lazy mount the floating panel, you can pass the `lazyMount` prop to the machine.\n\n**Example: lazy-mount**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { FloatingPanel } from '@ark-ui/react/floating-panel'\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport { ArrowDownLeft, GripVertical, Maximize2, Minus, XIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/floating-panel.module.css'\n\nexport const LazyMount = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cFloatingPanel.Root lazyMount onExitComplete={() =\u003e console.log('onExitComplete invoked')}\u003e\n    \u003cFloatingPanel.Trigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003eToggle Panel\u003c/FloatingPanel.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cPortal\u003e\n      \u003cFloatingPanel.Positioner className={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n        \u003cFloatingPanel.Content className={styles.Content}\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.DragTrigger\u003e\n            \u003cFloatingPanel.Header className={styles.Header}\u003e\n              \u003cFloatingPanel.Title className={styles.Title}\u003e\n                \u003cGripVertical /\u003e\n                Floating Panel\n              \u003c/FloatingPanel.Title\u003e\n              \u003cFloatingPanel.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n                \u003cFloatingPanel.StageTrigger stage=\"minimized\" className={styles.ControlButton}\u003e\n                  \u003cMinus /\u003e\n                \u003c/FloatingPanel.StageTrigger\u003e\n                \u003cFloatingPanel.StageTrigger stage=\"maximized\" className={styles.ControlButton}\u003e\n                  \u003cMaximize2 /\u003e\n                \u003c/FloatingPanel.StageTrigger\u003e\n                \u003cFloatingPanel.StageTrigger stage=\"default\" className={styles.ControlButton}\u003e\n                  \u003cArrowDownLeft /\u003e\n                \u003c/FloatingPanel.StageTrigger\u003e\n                \u003cFloatingPanel.CloseTrigger className={styles.ControlButton}\u003e\n                  \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n                \u003c/FloatingPanel.CloseTrigger\u003e\n              \u003c/FloatingPanel.Control\u003e\n            \u003c/FloatingPanel.Header\u003e\n          \u003c/FloatingPanel.DragTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.Body className={styles.Body}\u003e\n            \u003cp\u003eSome content\u003c/p\u003e\n          \u003c/FloatingPanel.Body\u003e\n\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"n\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"e\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"w\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"s\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"ne\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"se\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"sw\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"nw\" className={styles.ResizeTrigger} /\u003e\n        \u003c/FloatingPanel.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/FloatingPanel.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Portal\u003e\n  \u003c/FloatingPanel.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { FloatingPanel } from '@ark-ui/solid/floating-panel'\nimport { ArrowDownLeft, GripVertical, Maximize2, \u003c/FloatingPanel.StageTrigger\u003e\n                \u003cFloatingPanel.CloseTrigger :class=\"styles.ControlButton\"\u003e\n                  \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n \u003cFloatingPanel.Body :class=\"styles.Body\"\u003e\n            \u003cp\u003eSome content\u003c/p\u003e\n          \u003c/FloatingPanel.Body\u003e\n\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"n\" :class=\"styles.ResizeTrigger\" /\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"e\" :class=\"styles.ResizeTrigger\" /\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"w\" :class=\"styles.ResizeTrigger\" /\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"s\" :class=\"styles.ResizeTrigger\" /\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"ne\" :class=\"styles.ResizeTrigger\" /\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"se\" :class=\"styles.ResizeTrigger\" /\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"sw\" :class=\"styles.ResizeTrigger\" /\u003e\n          \u003cFloatingPanel.ResizeTrigger axis=\"nw\" :class=\"styles.ResizeTrigger\" /\u003e\n        \u003c/FloatingPanel.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/FloatingPanel.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Teleport\u003e\n  \u003c/FloatingPanel.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import `useFloatingPanelContext` hook or the\n`FloatingPanel.Context` component.\n\n**Example: context**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { FloatingPanel } from '@ark-ui/react/floating-panel'\nimport { Portal Panel\u003c/FloatingPanel.Trigger\u003e\n  \u003cFloatingPanel.Context\u003e\n    {#snippet render(floatingPanel)}\n      \u003cp\u003efloatingPanel is {floatingPanel().open ? \u003c/FloatingPanel.Positioner\u003e\n  \u003c/Portal\u003e\n\u003c/FloatingPanel.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n## API Reference\n\n### Props\n\n**Component API Reference**\n\n#### React\n\n**Root Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `allowOverflow` | `boolean` | No | Whether the panel should be strictly contained within the boundary when dragging |\n| `closeOnEscape` | `boolean` | No | Whether the panel should close when the escape key is pressed |\n| `defaultOpen` | `boolean` | No | The initial open state of the panel when rendered.\nUse when you don't need to control the open state of the panel. |\n| `defaultPosition` | `Point` | No | The initial position of the panel when rendered.\nUse when you don't need to control the position of the panel. |\n| `defaultSize` | `Size` | No | The default size of the panel |\n| `dir` | `'ltr' | 'rtl'` | No | The document's text/writing direction. |\n| `disabled` | `boolean` | No | Whether the panel is disabled |\n| `draggable` | `boolean` | No | Whether the panel is draggable |\n| `getAnchorPosition` | `(details: AnchorPositionDetails) =\u003e Point` | No | Function that returns the initial position of the panel when it is opened.\nIf provided, will be used instead of the default position. |\n| `getBoundaryEl` | `() =\u003e HTMLElement | null` | No | The boundary of the panel. Useful for recalculating the boundary rect when\nthe it is resized. |\n| `gridSize` | `number` | No | The snap grid for the panel |\n| `id` | `string` | No | The unique identifier of the machine. |\n| `ids` | `Partial\u003c{ trigger: string; positioner: string; content: string; title: string; header: string }\u003e` | No | The ids of the elements in the floating panel. Useful for composition. |\n| `immediate` | `boolean` | No | Whether to synchronize the present change immediately or defer it to the next frame |\n| `lazyMount` | `boolean` | No | Whether to enable lazy mounting |\n| `lockAspectRatio` | `boolean` | No | Whether the panel is locked to its aspect ratio |\n| `maxSize` | `Size` | No | The maximum size of the panel |\n| `minSize` | `Size` | No | The minimum size of the panel |\n| `onExitComplete` | `VoidFunction` | No | Function called when the animation ends in the closed state |\n| `onOpenChange` | `(details: OpenChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Function called when the panel is opened or closed |\n| `onPositionChange` | `(details: PositionChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Function called when the position of the panel changes via dragging |\n| `onPositionChangeEnd` | `(details: PositionChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Function called when the position of the panel changes via dragging ends |\n| `onSizeChange` | `(details: SizeChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Function called when the size of the panel changes via resizing |\n| `onSizeChangeEnd` | `(details: SizeChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Function called when the size of the panel changes via resizing ends |\n| `onStageChange` | `(details: StageChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Function called when the stage of the panel changes |\n| `open` | `boolean` | No | The controlled open state of the panel |\n| `persistRect` | `boolean` | No | Whether the panel size and position should be preserved when it is closed |\n| `position` | `Point` | No | The controlled position of the panel |\n| `present` | `boolean` | No | Whether the node is present (controlled by the user) |\n| `resizable` | `boolean` | No | Whether the panel is resizable |\n| `size` | `Size` | No | The size of the panel |\n| `skipAnimationOnMount` | `boolean` | No | Whether to allow the initial presence animation. |\n| `strategy` | `'absolute' | 'fixed'` | No | The strategy to use for positioning |\n| `translations` | `IntlTranslations` | No | The translations for the floating panel. |\n| `unmountOnExit` | `boolean` | No | Whether to unmount on exit. |\n\n\n**Body Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Body Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | floating-panel |\n| `[data-part]` | body |\n| `[data-dragging]` | Present when in the dragging state |\n| `[data-minimized]` | Present when minimized |\n| `[data-maximized]` | Present when maximized |\n| `[data-staged]` | Present when not in default stage |\n\n\n**CloseTrigger Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Content Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Content Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | floating-panel |\n| `[data-part]` | content |\n| `[data-state]` | \"open\" | \"closed\" |\n| `[data-dragging]` | Present when in the dragging state |\n| `[data-topmost]` | Present when topmost |\n| `[data-behind]` | Present when not topmost |\n| `[data-minimized]` | Present when minimized |\n| `[data-maximized]` | Present when maximized |\n| `[data-staged]` | Present when not in default stage |\n\n\n**Control Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Control Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | floating-panel |\n| `[data-part]` | control |\n| `[data-disabled]` | Present when disabled |\n| `[data-stage]` | The stage of the control |\n| `[data-minimized]` | Present when minimized |\n| `[data-maximized]` | Present when maximized |\n| `[data-staged]` | Present
